yeh kahani inho ne sirf ghanton mein mukammal kit hi
inayat hussain bhatti ki samaji khidmat bhi hain

ye film kuch itni kamyab hoi ye is ne salman khan ko raaton raat super star bana deya isi film ke leye salman khan ko behtareen naye adakar ka film fare award diya gaya jab ke isi ke sath un ko behtareen markazi kirdar ke leye bhi naamzad kiya gaya tha

ke awail mein andaz apna apna ne aik bar phir salman khan ko kamyabi ki shahrah par gamzan kar diya
mein hi release hone wali film hum aapke hain koun block buster sabit hoi is film ke hisse mein kai awards bhi aaye
